</td></tr>

<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1817, 1819 and 1826 (in 3 books)
</td></tr>

</th>

<span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_4_players&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 4 players</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_violin&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the violin</a></span>;
